                var autoHideBreakPoints = [{"width":0,"rWidth":1100,"autoHide":"scroll"},{"width":1100,"rWidth":9999,"autoHide":"never"}];
                var autoHide = autoHideBreakPoints.filter(function(item){
                    return window.innerWidth >= item.width && window.innerWidth < item.rWidth
                })[0].autoHide;
                
                
                var scrollbarInstance;
                var bodyScrollTop = document.body.scrollTop;
                var scrollTopDiff = 0;

                // 애니메이션 오브젝트 인스턴스
                var aniObjects = [];
                var addAnimation = function(elm,cn){
                    aniObjects.push({
                        elm:elm,
                        cn:cn
                    })
                }

                var isInViewport = function (elem) {
                    var bounding = elem.getBoundingClientRect();
                    return (
                        bounding.top >= 0 &&
                        bounding.bottom <= (window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight)
                    );
                };

                var updateAnimation = function(){
                    aniObjects = aniObjects.filter(function(obj){
                        var elm = obj.elm;
                        var cn = obj.cn;
                        if(isInViewport(elm)){
                            elm.addEventListener('animationend', function(){
                                //애니메이션 끝난후 처리
                                // elm.style.animationPlayState="pause";
                                elm.classList.add("animation-none");
                                // elm.classList.remove(cn); 
                                // elm.setAttribute("data-animation-backup",cn)
                            });
                            usingRaf(function(){
                                // elm.style.animationPlayState="paused";
                                elm.classList.remove("opacity0"); 
                                elm.classList.add(cn);
                                // elm.style.animationPlayState="unset";
                            })
                            return false;
                        }
                        return true;
                    });
                }
               
                //터치 이벤트 발생시 hover 모두 무효화
                document.addEventListener('touchstart', function addtouchclass(e) { // first time user touches the screen
                    document.body.classList.remove('no-touch') // add "can-touch" class to document root using classList API
                    document.removeEventListener('touchstart', addtouchclass, false) // de-register touchstart event
                }, false)

                var scrollListeners = {};
                var setScrollListener = function(key,func){
                    scrollListeners[key] = func;
                };
                var resizeListeners = {};
                var setResizeListener = function(key,func){
                    resizeListeners[key] = func;
                };
                window.addEventListener("resize",function(){
                    Object.keys(resizeListeners).forEach(function(key){
                        if(!resizeListeners[key]) return;
                        resizeListeners[key](event.target);
                    })
                });

                var findSectionByElm = function(elm){
                    var isSection = elm.classList.contains("section");
                    if(isSection) {
                        return elm;
                    }
                    if(elm ===document.body) {
                        return null;
                    }
                    return findSectionByElm(elm.parentElement);
                };
                
                //외부 스크립트
                

        function _init_toggle_section(id, defaultValue){
            var sect = document.getElementById(id);

            if(!defaultValue){
                sect.style.display="none";
            }else{
                sect.dispatchEvent(new Event("section-on"));
            }
        }

        function _action_toggle_section(on,off){
            on.forEach(function(id){
                var sect = document.getElementById("section-"+id);
                if(!sect) return;
                if(sect.style.display!=="none") return;
                sect.style.display="block";
                _objects_height_adjust("objects-"+id);
                sect.dispatchEvent(new Event("section-on"));
            });

            off.forEach(function(id){
                var sect = document.getElementById("section-"+id);
                if(!sect) return;
                if(sect.style.display==="none") return;
                sect.style.display="none";
                sect.dispatchEvent(new Event("section-off"));
            });
        }
        

            function _objects_height_adjust(id){
                var container  = document.getElementById(id);
                if(!container) return;
                var innerObjects = Array.from(container.children);
                
                var maxBottom = innerObjects.reduce(function(max, item){
                    var bottom = item.offsetTop + item.offsetHeight;
                    if (bottom > max) max = bottom;
                    return max;
                }, 0);
    
                if (container.clientHeight !== maxBottom) {
                    container.style.height = maxBottom + "px";
                }
            }

            function _objects_size_observe(id){
                var container  = document.getElementById(id);
                if(!container) return;
                var config = { attributes: true, subtree: true, childList: true };
                var observer = new MutationObserver(function (mutations) {
                    for (var i = 0; i < mutations.length; i++) {
                        var mutation = mutations[i];
                        if (mutation.attributeName === "style" || mutation.type === "childList") {
                            _objects_height_adjust(id);
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                });
                observer.observe(container, config);
            }

                    var documentWidth = documentRect.width;
                    var margin = -documentRect.left;

                    var left = margin;
                    var width = documentWidth;
                    
                    if (bodyWidth > documentWidth) {
                        width = bodyWidth;
                    }

                }

            function sendMail1839(){
                
                var fields = [{"id":"gdgAsLnQKQJwfggueQYeyg","type":"text","label":"이　　름","width":"90","required":true,"typeData":{"items":["항목1","항목2","항목3"],"placeholder":""},"showLabel":true,"letterSpacing":0},{"id":"kjZtXbQNg53wZSV3L8Fhut","type":"text","label":"전화번호","width":"90","required":true,"typeData":{"items":["항목1","항목2","항목3"],"placeholder":""},"showLabel":true},{"id":"352CVvFGF8XKgq1BWUs6vn","type":"textarea","label":"문의내용","width":"90","required":true,"typeData":{"items":["항목1"],"height":"150","placeholder":"문의 내용을 남겨주시면 더욱 자세한 답변을 받아보실 수 있습니다."},"showLabel":true}];
                if(!fields.length) return;

                fields.forEach(function(item){
                    item.elm = document.querySelector(".obj-1839-"+ item.id); 
                    item.inputElements = [].map.call(item.elm.querySelectorAll('input, textarea, select'),function(e){return e});

                    if(["text","textarea","select"].includes(item.type)){
                        item.value = item.inputElements[0].value;
                        item.textValue = item.value;
                    }else if(["check","option"].includes(item.type)){
                        item.value = item.inputElements.filter(function(elm){
                                        return elm.checked;
                                    }).map(function(elm){
                                        return elm.value;
                                    });
                        item.textValue = item.value.join(" , ");
                    }
                });

                var invalidInput = fields.find(function(item){
                    if(!item.required) return false;
                    if(["text","textarea","select"].includes(item.type)){
                        return !item.value;
                    }else if(["check","option"].includes(item.type)){
                        return item.value.length===0;
                    }
                });

                if(invalidInput){
                      swal({
                        text:invalidInput.label.replaceAll("　","")+"은(는) 필수입력입니다.",
                        button :"확인"
                    }).then(function(){
                        invalidInput.inputElements[0].select();
                    });
                    return;
                }

                
                    if(!document.getElementById('privacyCheck1839').checked){
                        swal({
                            text:'개인정보 취급방침 확인/동의가 필요합니다.',
                            button :"확인"
                        });
                        return;
                    }
                

                var ajaxData = {
                    to:"group1.ok114@gmail.com",
                    data:fields.reduce(function(acc,item){
                        acc[item.label] = item.textValue
                        return acc;
                    },{})
                }

                ajax_post('/formmail-log/1306',{content:ajaxData},
                function(){
                    console.log('forrmail_log');
                },function(){
                    console.warn('forrmail_log_failed');
                });

                var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
                xhr.onload = function () {
                    if (xhr.status === 200 || xhr.status === 201) {
                        
                        swal({
                            text:'문의가 접수되었습니다 :D',
                            button :"확인"
                        });

                        (function(){
                            if(window.onFormmailSendSuccess){
                                window.onFormmailSendSuccess(1839);
                            }
                        })();

                        fields.forEach(function(item){
                            if(["text","textarea"].includes(item.type)){
                                item.inputElements[0].value = '';
                            }else if(["check","option"].includes(item.type)){
                                item.inputElements.forEach(function(innerItem){
                                    innerItem.checked=false;
                                });
                            }
                        });
                        console.log(xhr.responseText);
                    } else {
                        swal({
                            text:'메일 전송을 실패했습니다.',
                            button :"확인"
                        });

                        console.error(xhr.responseText);
                    }
                };
                xhr.open('POST', 'https://public.webworx.co.kr/sendmail');
                xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
                xhr.send(JSON.stringify(ajaxData));

            }

                function _overlay_section_adjust(id){
                    function adjust(){
                        var section = document.getElementById(id);
                        var parentRect = section.parentNode.getBoundingClientRect();
                        section.style.opacity = "1";
                        section.style.width = parentRect.width + "px";
                        section.style.left = parentRect.left + "px";
                    }

                    adjust();
                    window.addEventListener("resize",function(){
                        adjust();
                    });
                }

var backup_css = {display:{},backgroundColor:{}};
function css_effect(selector,type,val){
var target = document.querySelector(selector);
var innerTarget = target.querySelector(".tr-ef-"+type);
target = innerTarget?innerTarget:target;
var backupValue = (backup_css[type]||{})[selector];
if(!backupValue){
if (!backup_css[type]) backup_css[type] = {};
backup_css[type][selector] = window.getComputedStyle(target)[type]
}

if(target.style[type]!==backupValue) target.style[type]=val;
}

function disable_css_effect(selector,type){
var target = document.querySelector(selector);
var innerTarget = target.querySelector(".tr-ef-"+type);
target = innerTarget?innerTarget:target;
if((backup_css[type]||{})[selector]){
target.style[type]= backup_css[type][selector];
delete backup_css[type][selector];
}
}
function reset_obj_trigger(id) {
var disable = function (listeners) {
return Object.keys(listeners).filter(function (key) {
var sp = key.split("_");
return sp[0] === "trigger" && Number(sp[1]) === id
})
.forEach(function (key) {
listeners[key](true);
delete listeners[key];
})
}
disable(resizeListeners);
disable(scrollListeners);
}

//트리거 값 변경되기 전의 위치를 기록하는 앵커 생성
function makeAnchorDom(){
var collection = {};
return {
add:function(id,elm){
var computed = window.getComputedStyle(elm);
var parent = elm.parentElement;

var div = document.createElement("DIV");
div.style.pointerEvents= "none";
div.style.left = computed.left;
div.style.top = computed.top;
div.style.width = computed.width;
div.style.height = computed.height;
div.style.position= computed.position;
parent.appendChild(div);

collection[id] = {
parent:parent,
div:div
}
},
has:function(id){
return !!collection[id];
},
get:function(id){
return collection[id].div;
},
delete:function(id){
var backup = collection[id];
if(!backup) return;
backup.parent.removeChild(backup.div);
delete collection[id];
}
}
}


function effect_show(selector){
disable_css_effect(selector,"display")

}
function disable_effect_show(selector){
css_effect(selector,"display","none");

var target = document.querySelector(selector);
if(!target) return;

[].forEach.call(
[target].concat(
Array.prototype.slice.call(
target.querySelectorAll(".animation-none")
)
),
function(el){
el.classList.remove("animation-none");
}
)
}



var stickyManager = (function () {

var targets = {};
function setTarget(id, elm, parent, verticalMargin, horizontalMargin, verticalLimitByParent) {
var anchorDiv = document.createElement("DIV");
var computed = window.getComputedStyle(elm)
anchorDiv.style.pointerEvents = "none";
anchorDiv.style.left = computed.left;
anchorDiv.style.top = computed.top;
anchorDiv.style.width = computed.width;
anchorDiv.style.height = computed.height;
anchorDiv.style.position = computed.position;
parent.appendChild(anchorDiv);

var backupParentZindex = parent.style.zIndex;
var backupParentPosition = parent.style.position;
var backupLeft = computed.left;
var backupTop = computed.top;
var backupPosition = computed.position;

var prevPosition = null;
targets[id] = {
getAnchorDiv: function () {
return anchorDiv;
},
unset: function () {
parent.removeChild(anchorDiv);
if (prevPosition) {
elm.style.left = backupLeft;
elm.style.top = backupTop;
elm.style.position = backupPosition;
parent.style.zIndex = backupParentZindex;
}
delete targets[id];
},
enable: function (position) {
if (prevPosition && prevPosition.left === position.left && prevPosition.top === position.top) return;
elm.style.position = "fixed";
parent.style.zIndex = 5000;
if (backupParentPosition === "static") parent.style.position = "relative";
if (position.top !== undefined) elm.style.top = position.top;
if (position.left !== undefined) elm.style.left = position.left;

prevPosition = {
top: position.top,
left: position.left
};
},
disable: function () {
if (!prevPosition) return;
elm.style.left = backupLeft;
elm.style.top = backupTop;
elm.style.position = backupPosition;
parent.style.zIndex = backupParentZindex;
parent.style.position = backupParentPosition;
prevPosition = null;
},
getElement: function () { return elm },
getParentElement: function () { return parent },
isLimitVerticalByParent: verticalLimitByParent,
verticalMargin: verticalMargin || 0,
horizontalMargin: horizontalMargin || 0
}
}

function checkOverflow(id) {
var anchorDiv = targets[id].getAnchorDiv();
var verticalMargin = targets[id].verticalMargin;
var horizontalMargin = targets[id].horizontalMargin;
var parent = targets[id].getParentElement();
var isLimitVertical = targets[id].isLimitVerticalByParent

var rect = anchorDiv.getBoundingClientRect();
var left = rect.left;
var top = rect.top;
var width = rect.width;
var height = rect.height;

var viewPortHeight = (window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight);
var viewPortWidth = (window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth);

var overLeft = (left - horizontalMargin) < 0;
var overTop = (top - verticalMargin) < 0;
var overRight = viewPortWidth < (left + width + horizontalMargin);
var overBottom = viewPortHeight < (top + height + verticalMargin);

if (!overTop && !overLeft && !overRight && !overBottom) {
targets[id].disable();
return;
}

var newPosition = {};


if (overTop) {
newPosition.top = verticalMargin;
if (isLimitVertical) {
var parentRect = parent.getBoundingClientRect();
if ((parentRect.top + parentRect.height) < (newPosition.top + height)) {
newPosition.top = parentRect.top + parentRect.height - height;
}
}
} else if (overBottom) {
newPosition.top = viewPortHeight - height - verticalMargin;
if (isLimitVertical) {
var parentRect = parent.getBoundingClientRect();
if (parentRect.top > newPosition.top) {
newPosition.top = parentRect.top;
}
}
} else {
newPosition.top = rect.top;
}
newPosition.top = newPosition.top + "px";

if (overLeft) {
newPosition.left = horizontalMargin;
} else if (overRight) {
newPosition.left = viewPortWidth - width - horizontalMargin;
} else {
newPosition.left = rect.left;
}
newPosition.left = newPosition.left + "px";

targets[id].enable(newPosition);
}

return {
enable: function (id, target, parent, verticalMargin, horizontalMargin, verticalLimitByParent) {
if (!targets[id]) {
if (!parent || !target) return;
setTarget(id, target, parent, verticalMargin, horizontalMargin, verticalLimitByParent);
}

checkOverflow(id);
},
disable: function (id) {
if (targets[id]) {
targets[id].unset();
delete targets[id];
}
},
checkOverflow:function(id) {
if(!targets[id]) return;
checkOverflow(id);
}
}
}());


function getSectionElm(elm) {
var target = elm;
while (!target.hasAttribute("data-section")) {
if (target.tagName === "BODY") {
return;
}
target = target.parentNode;
}
return target;
}


var effect_move_inside_flags = {};
function effect_move_inside(selector, marginX, marginY, boxTarget){
if(!effect_move_inside_flags[selector]){
var target = document.querySelector(selector);
var parent = getSectionElm(target);
if(!target || !parent) return;
var limitVertical = boxTarget==="section";
stickyManager.enable(selector, target, parent, marginY, marginX,limitVertical);
effect_move_inside_flags[selector] = true;
} else {
stickyManager.checkOverflow(selector);
}
}

function disable_effect_move_inside(selector){
stickyManager.disable(selector);
delete effect_move_inside_flags[selector];
}

function run(when){
var pass=[]
var selector = "#obj-1838";
var target = document.querySelector(selector);
if(!target) {
disable();
return;
}

pass.push(function(when){
var result = false;


let boundingTarget = target;
if(cond_outside_anchor.has(selector)){
boundingTarget = cond_outside_anchor.get(selector);
}

var rect = boundingTarget.getBoundingClientRect();
var left = rect.left;
var top = rect.top;
var width = rect.width;
var height = rect.height;

var viewPortHeight = (window.innerHeight || document.documentElement.clientHeight);
var viewPortWidth = (window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth);

var offsetY = undefined || 0;

var overPartX = viewPortWidth < (left + width)  || left < 0;
var overPartY = ((top - offsetY)   < 0) || (( top + height + offsetY)  > viewPortHeight);

var overFullX = viewPortWidth- left < 0 ||  (left + width) < 0;
var overFullY = (top + height) < 0 || top > viewPortHeight;

result = overFullX || overFullY


if(result && !cond_outside_anchor.has(selector)){
cond_outside_anchor.add(selector,target);
}else if(!result){
cond_outside_anchor.delete(selector);
}

return result;
})

if(pass.every(function(item){return (typeof item==='function')?item(when):item})){
effect_move_inside("#obj-1838",0,0, "viewport");
}
if(!pass.every(function(item){return (typeof item==='function')?item(when):item})){disable()}
}
setScrollListener("trigger_1838_chzpe6wNQgrUddDsg42YEK", function (remove) {
if (remove === true) {
disable();
} else {
run('scroll');
}
});
setResizeListener("trigger_1838_chzpe6wNQgrUddDsg42YEK", function (remove) {
if (remove === true) {
disable();
} else {
run('resize_window');
}
});

run('direct');

}

                outerResponsiveScript();
                
                // history.scrollRestoration = "manual";
                var smoothWheelInstance;
                document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
                    var isNaverApp = navigator.userAgent.indexOf("NAVER(inapp")> 0
                    // 스크롤바 활성
                    var prev;

                    if(!isNaverApp){
                        scrollbarInstance = OverlayScrollbars(document.querySelector('body'), {
                            overflowBehavior : {
                                x : "hidden",
                                y : "scroll"
                            },
                            scrollbars :{
                                autoHide:autoHide
                            },
                            callbacks : {
                                onInitialized:function(os){
                                    var self = this;
                                    var query = (function(){
                                                var queryString = location.href.split("?")[1];
                                                if(!queryString) return {};
                                                queryString = queryString.split("#")[0];
                                                return queryString.split("&").reduce(function(acc,item){
                                                    var splited = item.split("=");
                                                    if(splited.length < 2) return;
                                                    acc[splited[0]] = splited[1];
                                                    return acc;
                                                },{});
                                    })();
            
                                    (function(){
                                        if(!query.section) return;
                                        var target = document.getElementById("section-" + query.section);
                                        if(!target) return;
                                        
                                        usingRaf(function(){
                                            self.update(true);
                                            self.scroll({
                                                y:target.offsetTop
                                            })
                                            bodyScrollTop =target.offsetTop
                                        });
                                    })();
        
                                    usingRaf(function(){
                                        smoothWheelInstance = SmoothWheelScroll({
                                            element:document.querySelector("body .os-viewport"),
                                            speed: 120,
                                            smooth: 12
                                        });
                                    })
                                },
                                onScroll:function(event){
                                    smoothWheelInstance.updatePosition(bodyScrollTop);
                                    if(prev===event.target.scrollTop) return;
                                    prev = event.target.scrollTop;
                                    scrollTopDiff = event.target.scrollTop - bodyScrollTop;
                                    bodyScrollTop = event.target.scrollTop;
                                    Object.keys(scrollListeners).forEach(function(key){
                                        if(!scrollListeners[key]) return;
                                        scrollListeners[key](event.target);
                                    })
                                    updateAnimation();
                                }
                            }
                        });
                    }

                    if(isNaverApp){
                        scrollbarInstance = {
                            scroll: (param1, param2) => {
                            if (typeof param1 === 'string') return;
                                

                                const isElement = param1 instanceof HTMLElement;
                                const isNumber = typeof param1 === 'number'
                                const isObject = typeof param1 === 'object'

                                const scrollOptions = {
                                    behavior: 'smooth'
                                };

                                if (isNumber) {
                                    window.scrollTo({
                                        top: param1,
                                        ...scrollOptions
                                    });
                                    return;
                                }

                                if (isObject && isElement) {
                                    const targetElement = param1;
                                    targetElement.scrollIntoView(scrollOptions);
                                    return;
                                }

                                if (isObject && !isElement) {
                                    const y = param1.y;
                                    const el = param1.el;
                                    const margin = param1.margin;

                                    let top = 0;
                                    if (typeof y === 'string' && y.endsWith('%')) {
                                        const percent = parseFloat(y) / 100;
                                        top = document.documentElement.scrollHeight * percent;
                                    } else if (typeof y === 'number') {
                                        top = y;
                                    } else if (typeof y === 'object' && y instanceof HTMLElement) {
                                        top = y.offsetTop;
                                    } else if (el != null) {
                                        if (el) top = el.offsetTop;
                                    }


                                    if (margin != null) {
                                        console.log
                                        top = top - margin;
                                    }
                                    window.scrollTo({ top, ...scrollOptions });
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        document.body.style.overflow="auto"
                        document.body.style.overflowX="hidden"
                        var htmlDom = prod?document.querySelector("html"):document.body
                        window.addEventListener("scroll", function(){
                            if(prev===htmlDom.scrollTop) return;
                            prev = htmlDom.scrollTop;
                            scrollTopDiff = htmlDom.scrollTop - bodyScrollTop;
                            bodyScrollTop = htmlDom.scrollTop;
                            Object.keys(scrollListeners).forEach(function(key){
                                if(!scrollListeners[key]) return;
                                scrollListeners[key](htmlDom);
                            })
                            updateAnimation();
                        })
                     }
                    
                    //IE 스크롤 픽스
                    if (navigator.userAgent.match(/Trident\/7\./)) {
                        var scr = document.querySelector("body .os-viewport");
                        if(!scr){
                            src = window;
                        }
                        scr.addEventListener("mousewheel", function (event) {
                            event.preventDefault();
                            var wd = event.wheelDelta;
                            var csp = scr.scrollTop;
                            scrollbarInstance.scroll({y:csp - wd},0)
                        });
                    }
                    
                    // 전역 스크립트
                    
        var swiperSlides=[];
            function swiper_init(id, options){
                var slideObj =  swiperSlides[id];
                var objSelector ="#obj-"+id;
                var containerElm = document.querySelector(objSelector+" .swiper-container");

                // IE일경우 이펙트 변경
                if(isIE){
                    if(options.effect==="cube"){
                        options.effect="slide";
                    }
                }

                var siwperOptions = {
                    direction: options.direction,
                    loop: true,
                    pagination: {
                        el: objSelector + " .swiper-pagination"
                    },
                    navigation: {
                        nextEl: objSelector + " .swiper-button-next",
                        prevEl: objSelector + " .swiper-button-prev"
                    },
                    effect: options.effect || "slide",
                    cubeEffect: {
                        shadow: false
                    },
                    coverflowEffect: {
                        slideShadows: false
                    },
                    centeredSlides: true
                };

                if (options.centeredSlides !== undefined) {
                    siwperOptions.centeredSlides = options.centeredSlides;
                }

                if (options.delay) {
                    siwperOptions.autoplay = { delay: options.delay, disableOnInteraction: false };
                }

                // 멀티 슬라이드
                if (options.slidesPerView) {
                    siwperOptions.slidesPerView = options.slidesPerView;

                    //슬라이드 간의 간격
                    if (options.spaceBetween) {
                        siwperOptions.spaceBetween = options.spaceBetween;
                    }
                }

                if (slideObj) {
                    // 이전의 인덱스를 유지시켜준다
                    siwperOptions.initialSlide = slideObj.realIndex;
                    var backupCss = containerElm.style.cssText;
                    slideObj.destroy(false);
                    containerElm.style.cssText = backupCss;
                }

                    
                if(options.preventTouchMove){
                    siwperOptions.allowTouchMove = false;
                }
                swiperSlides[id] = new Swiper(containerElm, siwperOptions);
            }

            function slide_strip_instance(id){
                var obj = {
                    id:id,
                    listner:null
                }
                
                return {
                    setStrip:function(bool){
                        window.removeEventListener("resize",obj.listner); 
                        var elm = document.querySelector("#obj-"+obj.id+" .obj-slide");

                        if(bool){
                            var func = function(){
                                var doc = document.querySelector("#document");
                                elm.style.marginLeft = "-" + doc.getBoundingClientRect().left + "px";
                            }
                            func();
                            obj.listner = window.addEventListener("resize",func);
                        }else{
                            elm.style.marginLeft = 0;
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        

                var slide_strip_instance_1135 = slide_strip_instance(1135);
            

        function init_strip(id){
            var elm = document.querySelector("#obj-"+id+" .obj-strip");

            var func = function(){
                var doc = document.querySelector("#document");
                elm.style.marginLeft = "-" + doc.getBoundingClientRect().left + "px";
            }

            func();
            window.addEventListener("resize",func);
          }
        
        var strip_parallax_funcs = {};

        function strip_parallax(id,bool){
            var scr = document.querySelector("body .os-viewport");
            if(!scr){
                scr = window;
            }
            var elm = document.querySelector("#obj-"+id+" .strip-image"); 

            try{
                scr.removeEventListener("scroll",strip_parallax_funcs[id]);    
            }catch(e){}

            if(!bool) {
                if(!elm) return;
                elm.style.removeProperty('background-position-y');
                return;
            }
            
            var func = function () {
                if(!elm) return;
                var rect = elm.getBoundingClientRect();
                if (rect.top < window.innerHeight && rect.bottom > 0) {
                    var factor = rect.height / window.innerHeight;
                    var ratio = rect.top / (window.innerHeight - rect.height);
                    ratio = (((ratio * (1 - factor)) + (factor / 2)) * 100).toFixed(5);
                    elm.style.backgroundPositionY = ratio+"%";
                }
            }

            func();
            strip_parallax_funcs[id] = func;
            scr.addEventListener("scroll", strip_parallax_funcs[id])
        }

                function usingRaf(cb) {
                    return  window.requestAnimationFrame(cb)
                }

                    updateAnimation();

                function ajax_getOrDelete(url, callback, method) {
                    var request = new XMLHttpRequest();
                    request.open(method, url, true);
                    request.withCredentials = true;
                    request.onload = function() {
                        if (this.status >= 200 && this.status < 400) {
                            var resp = this.response;
                            callback(resp);
                        } else {
                            throw new Error(this);

                        }
                    };
                    request.onerror = function() {
                        throw new Error(this);
                    };
                    request.send();
                }

                function ajax_get(url, callback) {
                    ajax_getOrDelete(url, callback, "GET")
                }

                function ajax_post(url,data,success,failed){
                    var xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
                    
                    xhr.onload = function () {
                        if (xhr.status === 200 || xhr.status === 201) {
                            if(success) success(xhr.responseText);
                            console.log(xhr.responseText);
                        } else {
                            if(failed) failed(xhr.responseText);
                            console.error(xhr.responseText);
                        }
                    };

                    xhr.open('POST', url);
                    xhr.setRequestHeader('Content-Type', 'application/json');
                    xhr.send(JSON.stringify(data));
                }
                 

                //스크롤 부드럽게
        function SmoothWheelScroll(options) {
            var target = options.element;
            var speed = options.speed;
            var smooth = options.smooth;

            if (target === document)
                target = (document.scrollingElement
                    || document.documentElement
                    || document.body.parentNode
                    || document.body) // cross browser support for document scrolling

            var moving = false
            var pos = target.scrollTop;
            var frame = target === document.body
                && document.documentElement
                ? document.documentElement
                : target // safari is the new IE

            target.addEventListener('mousewheel', scrolled, { passive: false })


            function scrolled(e) {
                e.preventDefault(); // disable default scrolling

                var delta = normalizeWheelDelta(e)

                pos += -delta * speed
                pos = Math.max(0, Math.min(pos, target.scrollHeight - frame.clientHeight)) // limit scrolling

                if (!moving) update()
            }

            function normalizeWheelDelta(e) {
                if (e.detail) {
                    if (e.wheelDelta)
                        return e.wheelDelta / e.detail / 40 * (e.detail > 0 ? 1 : -1) // Opera
                    else
                        return -e.detail / 3 // Firefox
                } else
                    return e.wheelDelta / 120 // IE,Safari,Chrome
            }

            function update() {
                moving = true

                var delta = (pos - target.scrollTop) / smooth

                target.scrollTop += delta

                if (Math.abs(delta) > 1)
                    usingRaf(update)
                else
                    moving = false
            }

            return {
                stopMoving:function(){
                    moving = false;
                },
                updatePosition: function (paramPos) {
                    if (moving) return;
                    pos = paramPos;
                }
            }
        }

                </script>
